import os import re import requests # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with search...") # First search: General information about Pierpont-Bridgewater-Northern gang query1 = "Pierpont Bridgewater Northern gang John Dillinger bank robbery 1924 1934" max_results = 15 params1 = { "q": query1, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results } print(f"Searching for: {query1}") print("=" * 60) response1 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params1) if response1.status_code == 200: results1 = response1.json() if results1.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results1['organic_results'])} results for general gang search:") print() for i, result in enumerate(results1['organic_results'][:10], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"{i}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") print() else: print("No results found for general gang search") else: print(f"Error in first search: {response1.status_code} - {response1.text}") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n")

import os import re import requests # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with search...") # First search: General information about Pierpont-Bridgewater-Northern gang query1 = "Pierpont Bridgewater Northern gang John Dillinger bank robbery 1924 1934" max_results = 15 params1 = { "q": query1, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results } print(f"Searching for: {query1}") print("=" * 60) response1 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params1) if response1.status_code == 200: results1 = response1.json() if results1.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results1['organic_results'])} results for general gang search:") print() for i, result in enumerate(results1['organic_results'][:10], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"{i}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") print() else: print("No results found for general gang search") else: print(f"Error in first search: {response1.status_code} - {response1.text}") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n")

# Save the first search results and continue with targeted searches with open('workspace/search_results_1.txt', 'w') as f: f.write("SEARCH 1: General Pierpont-Bridgewater-Northern Gang Information\n") f.write("=" * 60 + "\n") f.write("Query: Pierpont Bridgewater Northern gang John Dillinger bank robbery 1924 1934\n\n") f.write("Key Findings from Initial Search:\n") f.write("- Harry Pierpont: Prohibition era gangster, convicted murderer, bank robber, mentor to Dillinger\n") f.write("- Everett Bridgewater: Early associate of Harry Pierpont, bank robber during Prohibition\n") f.write("- Earl Northern: Associate mentioned in bank robbery spree\n") f.write("- Gang suspected of at least 6 robberies, accused of robbing 24 banks and 4 other locations\n") f.write("- Dillinger paroled in May 1933, began robbing banks\n") f.write("- January 15, 1934: Bank robbery where police officer was killed\n") f.write("- January 21, 1934: Dillinger and 3 gang members arrived in Tucson\n\n") print("First search results saved. Continuing with targeted searches...") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n") # Second search: Focus on 1924 Indiana bank heist query2 = "Harry Pierpont Everett Bridgewater Earl Northern 1924 Indiana bank heist robbery first major" print(f"SEARCH 2: {query2}") print("=" * 60) params2 = { "q": query2, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 12 } response2 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params2) if response2.status_code == 200: results2 = response2.json() if results2.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results2['organic_results'])} results for 1924 Indiana heist:") print() for i, result in enumerate(results2['organic_results'][:8], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"{i}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") print() else: print("No results found for 1924 Indiana heist search") else: print(f"Error in second search: {response2.status_code}") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n") # Third search: Focus on 1934 black Hudson getaway car robbery query3 = "John Dillinger 1934 last bank robbery black Hudson getaway car Harry Pierpont" print(f"SEARCH 3: {query3}") print("=" * 60) params3 = { "q": query3, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 12 } response3 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params3) if response3.status_code == 200: results3 = response3.json() if results3.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results3['organic_results'])} results for 1934 black Hudson robbery:") print() for i, result in enumerate(results3['organic_results'][:8], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"{i}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") print() else: print("No results found for 1934 black Hudson robbery search") else: print(f"Error in third search: {response3.status_code}")

import os import requests # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with targeted searches...") # Save the previous search findings and continue with targeted searches with open('workspace/search_results_1.txt', 'w') as f: f.write("SEARCH 1: General Pierpont-Bridgewater-Northern Gang Information\n") f.write("=" * 60 + "\n") f.write("Query: Pierpont Bridgewater Northern gang John Dillinger bank robbery 1924 1934\n\n") f.write("Key Findings from Initial Search:\n") f.write("- Harry Pierpont: Prohibition era gangster, convicted murderer, bank robber, mentor to Dillinger\n") f.write("- Everett Bridgewater: Early associate of Harry Pierpont, bank robber during Prohibition\n") f.write("- Earl Northern: Associate mentioned in bank robbery spree\n") f.write("- Gang suspected of at least 6 robberies, accused of robbing 24 banks and 4 other locations\n") f.write("- Dillinger paroled in May 1933, began robbing banks\n") f.write("- January 15, 1934: Bank robbery where police officer was killed\n") f.write("- January 21, 1934: Dillinger and 3 gang members arrived in Tucson\n\n") print("First search results saved. import os import requests # Initialize API key and verify environment api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with comprehensive gang research...") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n") # Search 1: General Pierpont-Bridgewater-Northern gang information query1 = "\"Harry Pierpont\" \"Everett Bridgewater\" \"Earl Northern\" gang bank robbery Dillinger" print(f"SEARCH 1: {query1}") print("=" * 60) params1 = { "q": query1, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 15 } response1 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params1) if response1.status_code == 200: results1 = response1.json() if results1.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results1['organic_results'])} results for gang members search:") print() # Save and display results with open('workspace/gang_search_results.txt', 'w') as f: f.write("COMPREHENSIVE GANG RESEARCH RESULTS\n") f.write("=" * 50 + "\n\n") f.write("SEARCH 1: Gang Members - Harry Pierpont, Everett Bridgewater, Earl Northern\n") f.write("-" * 70 + "\n") for i, result in enumerate(results1['organic_results'][:10], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') link = result.get('link', 'No link') snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet') print(f"{i}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") print() f.write(f"{i}. {title}\n") f.write(f" URL: {link}\n") f.write(f" Snippet: {snippet}\n\n") else: print("No results found for gang members search") else: print(f"Error in first search: {response1.status_code} - {response1.text}") print("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n") # Python Code python
import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") exit() # Function to perform Google search def google_search(query, max_results=10): params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results, } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() return results.get("organic_results", []) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") return [] # Search queries focusing on key aspects search_queries = [ # Harry Pierpont murder trial for Sheriff Jess Sarber 'Harry Pierpont trial Sheriff Jess Sarber murder witness testimony 1933', 'Harry Pierpont conviction Jess Sarber Lima Ohio jail murder witness', 'Harry Pierpont trial testimony informant witness Sarber killing', # 1934 South Bend bank robbery (Dillinger's last) 'Dillinger South Bend bank robbery 1934 witness testimony trial', 'John Dillinger 1934 bank robbery conviction witness informant', 'South Bend robbery 1934 Dillinger gang witness testimony', # Cross-reference searches for common witnesses 'witness testified both Harry Pierpont Dillinger gang convictions', 'informant testimony Dillinger gang Pierpont murder trial', 'police informant Dillinger gang Harry Pierpont witness', 'accomplice turned state evidence Dillinger Pierpont testimony' ] all_results = {} print("Starting systematic search for witness/informant information...") print("=" * 70) for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f"\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 50) results = google_search(query, max_results=8) all_results[query] = results if results: for j, result in enumerate(results[:5], 1): # Show top 5 results print(f"{j}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}") print(f" URL: {result.get('link', 'No URL')}") if result.get('snippet'): print(f" Snippet: {result.get('snippet')[:200]}...") print() else: print("No results found for this query.") # Small delay between requests time.sleep(1) print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("SEARCH SUMMARY") print("=" * 70) total_results = sum(len(results) for results in all_results.values()) print(f"Total search queries executed: {len(search_queries)}") print(f"Total results retrieved: {total_results}") # Save all results to workspace for further analysis with open('workspace/witness_search_results.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\nAll search results saved to: workspace/witness_search_results.json") print("Next step: Analyze results for specific witness/informant names and cross-references")

import json import os # First, let's inspect the structure of the search results file results_file = 'workspace/witness_search_results.json' print("Inspecting the structure of witness search results...") print("=" * 60) if os.path.exists(results_file): with open(results_file, 'r') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f"File contains {len(data)} search queries") print("\nQuery keys in the file:") for i, query in enumerate(data.keys(), 1): print(f"{i}. {query}") # Check the structure of one result to understand the format first_query = list(data.keys())[0] first_results = data[first_query] print(f"\nStructure analysis for first query: '{first_query}'") print(f"Number of results: {len(first_results)}") if first_results: print("\nSample result structure:") sample_result = first_results[0] print(f"Keys in each result: {list(sample_result.keys())}") # Show a sample result print("\nSample result:") print(f"Title: {sample_result.get('title', 'N/A')}") print(f"Link: {sample_result.get('link', 'N/A')}") print(f"Snippet: {sample_result.get('snippet', 'N/A')[:100]}...") else: print("Results file not found. Need to run search first.") print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("Now analyzing all results for key witness names...") print("=" * 60) # Now let's analyze all results for witness/informant names key_witnesses = {} witness_keywords = [ 'Ed Shouse', 'Edward Shouse', 'Shouse', 'Wilbur Sharp', 'Sharp', 'Lucy Sarber', 'Sarber', 'witness', 'testified', 'testimony', 'informant', 'turned state', 'state evidence', 'accomplice', 'material witness' ] if os.path.exists(results_file): with open(results_file, 'r') as f: all_data = json.load(f) # Analyze each search query's results for query, results in all_data.items(): print(f"\nAnalyzing query: {query}") print("-" * 50) relevant_results = [] for result in results: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', '') # Check if any witness keywords appear in title or snippet combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() found_keywords = [] for keyword in witness_keywords: if keyword.lower() in combined_text: found_keywords.append(keyword) if found_keywords: relevant_results.append({ 'title': title, 'link': link, 'snippet': snippet, 'keywords_found': found_keywords }) if relevant_results: print(f"Found {len(relevant_results)} relevant results:") for i, result in enumerate(relevant_results, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['link']}") print(f" Keywords found: {', '.join(result['keywords_found'])}") print(f" Snippet: {result['snippet'][:200]}...") else: print("No results with witness keywords found.") print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("KEY FINDINGS SUMMARY") print("=" * 60) # Extract and summarize key witness information key_findings = [] if os.path.exists(results_file): with open(results_file, 'r') as f: all_data = json.load(f) # Look for specific mentions of Ed Shouse and other key witnesses ed_shouse_mentions = [] other_witnesses = [] for query, results in all_data.items(): for result in results: snippet = result.get('snippet', '') title = result.get('title', '') combined = f"{title} {snippet}" # Check for Ed Shouse specifically if 'shouse' in combined.lower(): ed_shouse_mentions.append({ 'query': query, 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': result.get('link', '') }) # Check for other witness names if any(name in combined.lower() for name in ['wilbur sharp', 'lucy sarber']): other_witnesses.append({ 'query': query, 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': result.get('link', '') }) print(f"ED SHOUSE MENTIONS ({len(ed_shouse_mentions)} found):") for mention in ed_shouse_mentions: print(f"\n• Title: {mention['title']}") print(f" Query: {mention['query']}") print(f" Snippet: {mention['snippet']}") print(f" URL: {mention['link']}") print(f"\nOTHER WITNESS MENTIONS ({len(other_witnesses)} found):") for mention in other_witnesses: print(f"\n• Title: {mention['title']}") print(f" Query: {mention['query']}") print(f" Snippet: {mention['snippet']}") print(f" URL: {mention['link']}") # Save analysis results analysis_results = { 'ed_shouse_mentions': ed_shouse_mentions if 'ed_shouse_mentions' in locals() else [], 'other_witnesses': other_witnesses if 'other_witnesses' in locals() else [], 'analysis_date': '2024', 'total_queries_analyzed': len(all_data) if 'all_data' in locals() else 0 } with open('workspace/witness_analysis.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\nAnalysis results saved to: workspace/witness_analysis.json")

import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") exit() # Function to perform Google search def google_search(query, max_results=10): params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results, } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() return results.get("organic_results", []) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}: {response.text}") return [] print("FOCUSED SEARCH: Ed Shouse and Cross-Case Testimony") print("=" * 60) print("Based on previous findings, Ed Shouse was identified as a key witness.") print("Now searching for evidence of his testimony in BOTH cases...\n") # Targeted searches focusing on Ed Shouse and cross-case connections focused_queries = [ # Ed Shouse specific searches '"Ed Shouse" testimony Harry Pierpont Dillinger gang witness', '"Edward Shouse" former gang member testified Pierpont Sarber murder', '"Ed Shouse" Dillinger gang informant South Bend bank robbery 1934', '"Ed Shouse" witness testimony both Pierpont Dillinger convictions', # Cross-case witness searches 'witness testified Pierpont Sarber murder AND Dillinger South Bend robbery', 'informant testimony Sheriff Sarber murder Dillinger 1934 bank robbery', 'same witness Pierpont murder trial Dillinger gang robbery conviction', # Court records and trial testimony searches 'Lima Ohio court records Harry Pierpont trial Ed Shouse testimony 1934', 'South Bend bank robbery 1934 trial witnesses informants testimony', 'federal trial Dillinger gang 1934 witnesses Ed Shouse testimony' ] all_focused_results = {} for i, query in enumerate(focused_queries, 1): print(f"Search {i}/{len(focused_queries)}: {query}") print("-" * 50) results = google_search(query, max_results=8) all_focused_results[query] = results if results: for j, result in enumerate(results[:4], 1): # Show top 4 results print(f"{j}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}") print(f" URL: {result.get('link', 'No URL')}") if result.get('snippet'): snippet = result.get('snippet') # Highlight key terms in snippet key_terms = ['Ed Shouse', 'Edward Shouse', 'Shouse', 'testimony', 'witness', 'informant', 'South Bend', 'Sarber'] for term in key_terms: if term.lower() in snippet.lower(): snippet = snippet.replace(term, f"**{term}**") print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:250]}...") print() else: print("No results found for this query.") # Small delay between requests time.sleep(1) print("\n" + "=" * 60) print("DETAILED ANALYSIS: Ed Shouse Cross-Case Evidence") print("=" * 60) # Analyze results for Ed Shouse cross-case connections ed_shouse_evidence = [] south_bend_witnesses = [] cross_case_evidence = [] for query, results in all_focused_results.items(): for result in results: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', '') combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() # import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") exit() print("INVESTIGATING ED SHOUSE: Cross-Case Witness Analysis") print("=" * 70) print("Goal: Determine if Ed Shouse testified in BOTH Pierpont murder AND Dillinger robbery cases") print("\nFrom previous research, we know:") print("- Ed Shouse was a former Dillinger gang member") print("- He testified against Harry Pierpont in the Sheriff Sarber murder trial (March 1934)") print("- We need to find if he also testified in Dillinger's 1934 South Bend robbery case") print("\n" + "=" * 70) # Function to perform Google search with error handling def google_search(query, max_results=8): try: params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results, } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() return results.get("organic_results", []) else: print(f"Error: API request failed with status {response.status_code}") return [] except Exception as e: print(f"Search error for query '{query}': {str(e)}") return [] # Specific searches to find Ed Shouse's role in both cases targeted_searches = [ # Ed Shouse and Pierpont trial (we know this exists) 'Ed Shouse testified Harry Pierpont trial Sheriff Sarber murder 1934', 'Edward Shouse witness testimony Pierpont Makley Clark Lima Ohio trial', # Highlight key terms highlighted_snippet = snippet key_terms = ['Ed Shouse', 'Edward Shouse', 'Shouse', 'South Bend', 'testimony', 'witness', 'testified'] for term in key_terms: if term.lower() in snippet.lower(): highlighted_snippet = highlighted_snippet.replace(term, f"**{term}**") print(f" Snippet: {highlighted_snippet[:300]}...") print() else: print("No results found for this query.") search_summary.append({ 'query': query, 'total_results': len(results), 'relevant_results': relevant_count }) # import os import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import json import time # Get SerpAPI key from environment variables api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key is None: print("Error: Missing API key. Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") exit() print("FINAL INVESTIGATION: Cross-Case Witness Analysis") print("=" * 70) print("Based on previous research findings:") print("- Ed Shouse confirmed as witness in Harry Pierpont's murder trial (Sheriff Sarber)") print("- Need to determine if Ed Shouse or ANY witness testified in BOTH cases") print("- Focus on 1934 South Bend bank robbery witness testimony") print("\n" + "=" * 70) # Function to perform Google search with proper error handling def safe_google_search(query, max_results=6): try: params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": max_results, } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params, timeout=30) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() return results.get("organic_results", []) else: print(f"API request failed with status {response.status_code}") return [] except Exception as e: print(f"Search error: {str(e)}") return [] # Final targeted searches to resolve the cross-case witness question final_searches = [ # Direct searches for Ed Shouse in South Bend case '"Ed Shouse" "South Bend" bank robbery 1934 testimony witness', '"Edward Shouse" "Merchants National Bank" South Bend June 1934', # Alternative witnesses who might have testified in both cases 'witness testified "Sheriff Sarber murder" "South Bend bank robbery" 1934', 'informant testimony "Harry Pierpont trial" "Dillinger South Bend robbery"', # Federal court records and cross-case testimony 'federal trial 1934 Dillinger gang witness "testified against both"', 'court records witness testimony "Pierpont conviction" "Dillinger robbery conviction"', # Gang members who turned state's evidence '"gang member" "turned state evidence" testified Pierpont Dillinger 1934', 'accomplice informant testimony "both Pierpont and Dillinger" convictions' ] all_final_results = {} key_evidence = [] for i, query in enumerate(final_searches, 1): print(f"\nFinal Search {i}/{len(final_searches)}: {query}") print("-" * 60) results = safe_google_search(query) all_final_results[query] = results if results: for j, result in enumerate(results[:4], 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') link = result.get('link', 'No URL') # Check for key evidence combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() is_key_evidence = False evidence_type = [] # Check for Ed Shouse mentions if any(term in combined_text for term in ['ed shouse', 'edward shouse']): evidence_type.append('Ed Shouse') is_key_evidence = True # Check for cross-case connections if (('pierpont' in combined_text or 'sarber' in combined_text) and ('south bend' in combined_text)): evidence_type.append('Cross-case connection') is_key_evidence = True # Check for witness/testimony mentions if any(term in combined_text for term in ['witness', 'testimony', 'testified']): evidence_type.append('Witness testimony') if is_key_evidence: key_evidence.append({ 'query': query, 'title': title, 'snippet': snippet, 'link': link, 'evidence_types': evidence_type }) print(f"*** {j}. {title} [KEY EVIDENCE: {', '.join(evidence_type)}]") else: print(f"{j}. {title}") print(f" URL: {link}") if snippet: print(f" Snippet: {snippet[:250]}...") print() else: print("No results found for this query.") time.sleep(2) # Longer delay to avoid issues print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("KEY EVIDENCE ANALYSIS") print("=" * 70) # Analyze key evidence found ed_shouse_south_bend = [] cross_case_witnesses = [] other_key_evidence = [] for evidence in key_evidence: if 'Ed Shouse' in evidence['evidence_types']: if 'south bend' in evidence['snippet'].lower(): ed_shouse_south_bend.append(evidence) else: other_key_evidence.append(evidence) elif 'Cross-case connection' in evidence['evidence_types']: cross_case_witnesses.append(evidence) else: other_key_evidence.append(evidence) print(f"\nED SHOUSE + SOUTH BEND EVIDENCE ({len(ed_shouse_south_bend)} found):") if ed_shouse_south_bend: for i, evidence in enumerate(ed_shouse_south_bend, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {evidence['title']}") print(f" Query: {evidence['query']}") print(f" Evidence Types: {', '.join(evidence['evidence_types'])}") print(f" Snippet: {evidence['snippet'][:300]}...") print(f" URL: {evidence['link']}") else: print("\n*** NO EVIDENCE FOUND of Ed Shouse testifying in South Bend robbery case ***") print(f"\nCROSS-CASE WITNESS EVIDENCE ({len(cross_case_witnesses)} found):") if cross_case_witnesses: for i, evidence in enumerate(cross_case_witnesses, 1): print(f"\n{i}. {evidence['title']}") print(f" Query: {evidence['query']}") print(f" Evidence Types: {', '.join(evidence['evidence_types'])}") print(f" Snippet: {evidence['snippet'][:300]}...") print(f" URL: {evidence['link']}") else: print("\n*** NO CROSS-CASE WITNESS EVIDENCE FOUND ***") print(f"\nOTHER KEY EVIDENCE ({len(other_key_evidence)} found):") for i, evidence in enumerate(other_key_evidence[:3], 1): # Show top 3 print(f"\n{i}. {evidence['title']}") print(f" Evidence Types: {', '.join(evidence['evidence_types'])}") print(f" Snippet: {evidence['snippet'][:200]}...") # Save final comprehensive analysis final_investigation_results = { 'investigation_type': 'Final cross-case witness analysis', 'search_queries': final_searches, 'ed_shouse_south_bend_evidence': ed_shouse_south_bend, 'cross_case_witness_evidence': cross_case_witnesses, 'other_key_evidence': other_key_evidence, 'total_key_evidence_found': len(key_evidence), 'total_searches_conducted': len(final_searches), 'investigation_date': '2024' } with open('workspace/final_cross_case_investigation.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(final_investigation_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\n\nFinal investigation results saved to: workspace/final_cross_case_investigation.json") # DEFINITIVE CONCLUSION print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("DEFINITIVE INVESTIGATION CONCLUSION") print("=" * 70) print("\nBASED ON COMPREHENSIVE RESEARCH:") print("\n1. ED SHOUSE TESTIMONY CONFIRMED:") print(" - Ed Shouse was a former Dillinger gang member") print(" - He testified against Harry Pierpont in the Sheriff Sarber murder trial (March 1934)") print(" - His testimony helped convict Pierpont, Makley, and Clark") print("\n2. SOUTH BEND ROBBERY WITNESS SEARCH:") if len(ed_shouse_south_bend) > 0: print(" - EVIDENCE FOUND: Ed Shouse also testified in South Bend robbery case") print(" - Ed Shouse is the cross-case witness we were looking for") elif len(cross_case_witnesses) > 0: print(" - ALTERNATIVE WITNESS FOUND: Another witness testified in both cases") print(" - Cross-case witness identified (not Ed Shouse)") else: print(" - NO EVIDENCE FOUND: Ed Shouse did not testify in South Bend robbery case") print(" - NO ALTERNATIVE CROSS-CASE WITNESS FOUND in available sources") print("\n3. FINAL ANSWER:") if len(ed_shouse_south_bend) > 0: print(" *** ED SHOUSE is the witness whose testimony led to convictions of both gang leaders ***") print(" - Testified against Harry Pierpont for Sheriff Sarber's murder") print(" - Also testified in Dillinger's 1934 South Bend bank robbery case") elif len(cross_case_witnesses) > 0: print(" *** CROSS-CASE WITNESS IDENTIFIED (review evidence above) ***") else: print(" *** NO DEFINITIVE CROSS-CASE WITNESS FOUND ***") print(" - Ed Shouse confirmed only for Pierpont case") print(" - Available sources do not show same witness testifying in both cases") print(" - May require access to actual court records or trial transcripts") print("\n" + "=" * 70) print("INVESTIGATION COMPLETE") print("=" * 70)

Make sure you have SERPAPI_API_KEY in your environment variables.") else: print("API key found, proceeding with searches...") # Search 1: Mary Kinder testimony Harry Pierpont trial query1 = '"Mary Kinder" "Harry Pierpont" testimony trial murder Sheriff Sarber' params1 = { "q": query1, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10 } print(f"\n=== SEARCH 1: Mary Kinder and Harry Pierpont Trial ===") print(f"Query: {query1}") response1 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params1) if response1.status_code == 200: results1 = response1.json() if results1.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results1['organic_results'])} results for Mary Kinder and Harry Pierpont trial:") for i, result in enumerate(results1['organic_results'][:5], 1): print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}") print(f" URL: {result.get('link', 'No URL')}") print(f" Snippet: {result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')}") else: print("No results found for Mary Kinder and Harry Pierpont trial") else: print(f"Error in search 1: {response1.status_code} - {response1.text}") # Search 2: Mary Kinder Dillinger gang informant witness query2 = '"Mary Kinder" Dillinger gang informant witness testimony court records 1934' params2 = { "q": query2, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 10 } print(f"\n\n=== SEARCH 2: Mary Kinder as Dillinger Gang Informant ===") print(f"Query: {query2}") response2 = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params2) if response2.status_code == 200: results2 = response2.json() if results2.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results2['organic_results'])} results for Mary Kinder as Dillinger informant:") for i, result in enumerate(results2['organic_results'][:5], 1): print(f"\n{i}. {result.get('title', 'No title')}") print(f" URL: {result.get('link', 'No URL')}") print(f" Snippet: {result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')}") else: print("No results found for Mary Kinder as Dillinger informant") else: print(f"Error in search 2: {response2.status_code} - import json import os # First, let's inspect the structure of the saved search results results_file = 'workspace/mary_kinder_search_results.json' print("=== INSPECTING SEARCH RESULTS FILE STRUCTURE ===") if os.path.exists(results_file): with open(results_file, 'r') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print(f"File exists and loaded successfully") print(f"Top-level keys: {list(search_data.keys())}") # Inspect structure of each search category for category, results in search_data.items(): print(f"\n{category}:") print(f" - Number of results: {len(results)}") if results: print(f" - Sample result keys: {list(results[0].keys())}") print(f" - Sample title: {results[0].get('title', 'No title')}") else: print(f"File {results_file} does not exist") print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR MARY KINDER TESTIMONY ===") # Now let's analyze the results for specific information about Mary Kinder's testimony key_findings = [] all_results = [] # Combine all results for comprehensive analysis for category, results in search_data.items(): for result in results: result['search_category'] = category all_results.append(result) print(f"\nTotal results across all searches: {len(all_results)}") # Look for specific keywords related to testimony, trials, and court records testimony_keywords = ['testimony', 'trial', 'court', 'witness', 'evidence', 'arraigned', 'murder', 'convicted'] informant_keywords = ['informant', 'state evidence', 'cooperation', 'FBI', 'federal'] pierpont_keywords = ['Pierpont', 'Sheriff Sarber', 'Lima', 'murder trial'] dillinger_keywords = ['Dillinger', 'South Bend', 'bank robbery', 'gang'] print("\n=== RELEVANT RESULTS ANALYSIS ===") for i, result in enumerate(all_results, 1): title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') url = result.get('link', '') category = result.get('search_category', '') # Check for testimony-related content combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() has_testimony = any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in testimony_keywords) has_informant = any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in informant_keywords) has_pierpont = any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in pierpont_keywords) has_dillinger = any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in dillinger_keywords) if has_testimony or has_informant or 'mary kinder' in combined_text: print(f"\n--- RESULT {i} [{category}] ---") print(f"Title: {title}") print(f"URL: {url}") print(f"Snippet: {snippet}") # Highlight key findings findings = [] if has_testimony: findings.append("Contains testimony/trial references") if has_informant: findings.append("Contains informant/evidence references") if has_pierpont: findings.append("References Pierpont case") if has_dillinger: findings.append("References Dillinger case") if findings: print(f"Key findings: {', '.join(findings)}") key_findings.extend(findings) print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== MOST PROMISING SOURCES FOR DETAILED INVESTIGATION ===") # Identify the most promising sources promising_sources = [] for result in all_results: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') url = result.get('link', '') # Prioritize sources that mention both Mary Kinder and legal proceedings combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() score = 0 reasons = [] if 'mary kinder' in combined_text: score += 2 reasons.append('Mentions Mary Kinder') if any(word in combined_text for word in ['testimony', 'trial', 'court', 'arraigned']): score += 3 reasons.append('Legal proceedings') if any(word in combined_text for word in ['pierpont', 'sarber']): score += 2 reasons.append('Pierpont/Sarber case') if any(word in combined_text for word in ['dillinger', 'south bend']): score += 2 reasons.append('Dillinger case') if 'archive.org' in url or 'newspapers.library' in url or '.gov' in url: score += 2 reasons.append('Primary/archival source') if score >= 4: promising_sources.append({ 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'score': score, 'reasons': reasons }) # Sort by score promising_sources.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True) print(f"\nFound {len(promising_sources)} high-priority sources:") for i, source in enumerate(promising_sources[:8], 1): # Top 8 sources print(f"\n{i}. {source['title']} (Score: {source['score']})") print(f" URL: {source['url']}") print(f" Reasons: {', '.join(source['reasons'])}") print(f" Snippet: {source['snippet'][:200]}...") # Save analysis results analysis_results = { 'total_results': len(all_results), 'key_findings_summary': list(set(key_findings)), 'promising_sources': promising_sources, 'next_steps': [ 'Examine archival sources (archive.org, newspapers.library.in.gov)', 'Focus on Indianapolis Times October 1934 article mentioning Mary Kinder visiting Harry Pierpont', 'Investigate FBI files and court records mentioned in search results', 'Look into Mary Kinder as potential state witness/informant', 'Cross-reference with Dillinger gang documentation' ] } with open('workspace/mary_kinder_analysis.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\n\n=== SUMMARY ===") print(f"Analysis saved to workspace/mary_kinder_analysis.json") print(f"Key findings: {', '.join(set(key_findings))}") print(f"Next step: Examine the {len(promising_sources)} most promising sources for detailed testimony information")

import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time import json print("=== EXAMINING TOP ARCHIVAL SOURCES FOR MARY KINDER TESTIMONY ===") # Let's start with the most promising archival sources identified in our analysis # Focus on primary sources that are likely to contain actual testimony details headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } findings = [] # Source 1: Indianapolis Times October 17, 1934 - newspaper archive print("\n=== SOURCE 1: Indianapolis Times October 17, 1934 ===") url1 = "https://newspapers.library.in.gov/?a=d&d=IPT19341017.1.1&" print(f"URL: {url1}") try: response1 = requests.get(url1, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response1.status_code == 200: soup1 = BeautifulSoup(response1.content, 'html.parser') # Look for text content related to Mary Kinder text1 = soup1.get_text() # Search for Mary Kinder mentions if 'mary kinder' in text1.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in this newspaper") # Extract relevant paragraphs lines = text1.split('\n') relevant_lines = [] for i, line in enumerate(lines): if 'mary kinder' in line.lower() or 'pierpont' in line.lower(): # Include context lines start = max(0, i-2) end = min(len(lines), i+3) relevant_lines.extend(lines[start:end]) if relevant_lines: relevant_text = '\n'.join(relevant_lines[:500]) # Limit output print(f"Relevant content:\n{relevant_text}") findings.append({ 'source': 'Indianapolis Times Oct 17 1934', 'url': url1, 'content': relevant_text, 'type': 'newspaper_archive' }) else: print("No Mary Kinder references found in accessible content") else: print(f"Could not access newspaper archive (Status: {response1.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing newspaper: {str(e)}") time.sleep(2) # Be respectful to servers # Source 2: FBI Archive - John Dillinger Gang files print("\n\n=== SOURCE 2: FBI Archive - John Dillinger Gang Files ===") url2 = "https://archive.org/stream/JohnDillingerGang/John%20Dillinger%20Gang%2011_djvu.txt" print(f"URL: {url2}") try: response2 = requests.get(url2, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response2.status_code == 200: fbi_text = response2.text print(f"FBI document loaded successfully ({len(fbi_text)} characters)") # Search for Mary Kinder references in FBI files if 'mary kinder' in fbi_text.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in FBI files") # Extract sections mentioning Mary Kinder lines = fbi_text.split('\n') mary_kinder_sections = [] for i, line in enumerate(lines): if 'mary kinder' in line.lower(): # Get surrounding context start = max(0, i-5) end = min(len(lines), i+10) section = '\n'.join(lines[start:end]) mary_kinder_sections.append(section) print(f"Found {len(mary_kinder_sections)} sections mentioning Mary Kinder:") for j, section in enumerate(mary_kinder_sections[:3], 1): # Show first 3 sections print(f"\n--- FBI Section {j} ---") print(section[:800] + "..." if len(section) > 800 else section) findings.append({ 'source': 'FBI John Dillinger Gang Files', 'url': url2, 'content': mary_kinder_sections, 'type': 'fbi_archive', 'sections_found': len(mary_kinder_sections) }) else: print("No Mary Kinder references found in FBI text") else: print(f"Could not access FBI archive (Status: {response2.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing FBI archive: {str(e)}") time.sleep(2) # Source 3: Indiana History Blog - Marion tag (government source) print("\n\n=== SOURCE 3: Indiana History Blog - Marion ===") url3 = "https://blog.history.in.gov/tag/marion/" print(f"URL: {url3}") try: response3 = requests.get(url3, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response3.status_code == 200: soup3 = BeautifulSoup(response3.content, 'html.parser') text3 = soup3.get_text() if 'mary kinder' in text3.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in Indiana History Blog") # Look for specific posts or articles articles = soup3.find_all(['article', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and ('post' in x.lower() or 'entry' in x.lower())) relevant_articles = [] for article in articles: article_text = article.get_text() if 'mary kinder' in article_text.lower(): relevant_articles.append(article_text[:1000]) # import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import time import json print("=== EXAMINING TOP ARCHIVAL SOURCES FOR MARY KINDER TESTIMONY ===") # Let's start with the most promising archival sources identified in our analysis # Focus on primary sources that are likely to contain actual testimony details headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } findings = [] # Source 1: Indianapolis Times October 17, 1934 - newspaper archive print("\n=== SOURCE 1: Indianapolis Times October 17, 1934 ===") url1 = "https://newspapers.library.in.gov/?a=d&d=IPT19341017.1.1&" print(f"URL: {url1}") try: response1 = requests.get(url1, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response1.status_code == 200: soup1 = BeautifulSoup(response1.content, 'html.parser') # Look for text content related to Mary Kinder text1 = soup1.get_text() # Search for Mary Kinder mentions if 'mary kinder' in text1.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in this newspaper") # Extract relevant paragraphs lines = text1.split('\n') relevant_lines = [] for i, line in enumerate(lines): if 'mary kinder' in line.lower() or 'pierpont' in line.lower(): # Include context lines start = max(0, i-2) end = min(len(lines), i+3) relevant_lines.extend(lines[start:end]) if relevant_lines: relevant_text = '\n'.join(relevant_lines[:500]) # Limit output print(f"Relevant content:\n{relevant_text}") findings.append({ 'source': 'Indianapolis Times Oct 17 1934', 'url': url1, 'content': relevant_text, 'type': 'newspaper_archive' }) else: print("No Mary Kinder references found in accessible content") else: print(f"Could not access newspaper archive (Status: {response1.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing newspaper: {str(e)}") time.sleep(2) # Be respectful to servers # Source 2: FBI Archive - John Dillinger Gang files print("\n\n=== SOURCE 2: FBI Archive - John Dillinger Gang Files ===") url2 = "https://archive.org/stream/JohnDillingerGang/John%20Dillinger%20Gang%2011_djvu.txt" print(f"URL: {url2}") try: response2 = requests.get(url2, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response2.status_code == 200: fbi_text = response2.text print(f"FBI document loaded successfully ({len(fbi_text)} characters)") # Search for Mary Kinder references in FBI files if 'mary kinder' in fbi_text.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in FBI files") # Extract sections mentioning Mary Kinder lines = fbi_text.split('\n') mary_kinder_sections = [] for i, line in enumerate(lines): if 'mary kinder' in line.lower(): # Get surrounding context start = max(0, i-5) end = min(len(lines), i+10) section = '\n'.join(lines[start:end]) mary_kinder_sections.append(section) print(f"Found {len(mary_kinder_sections)} sections mentioning Mary Kinder:") for j, section in enumerate(mary_kinder_sections[:3], 1): # Show first 3 sections print(f"\n--- FBI Section {j} ---") print(section[:800] + "..." if len(section) > 800 else section) findings.append({ 'source': 'FBI John Dillinger Gang Files', 'url': url2, 'content': mary_kinder_sections, 'type': 'fbi_archive', 'sections_found': len(mary_kinder_sections) }) else: print("No Mary Kinder references found in FBI text") else: print(f"Could not access FBI archive (Status: {response2.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing FBI archive: {str(e)}") time.sleep(2) # Source 3: Indiana History Blog - Marion tag (government source) print("\n\n=== SOURCE 3: Indiana History Blog - Marion ===") url3 = "https://blog.history.in.gov/tag/marion/" print(f"URL: {url3}") try: response3 = requests.get(url3, headers=headers, timeout=30) if response3.status_code == 200: soup3 = BeautifulSoup(response3.content, 'html.parser') text3 = soup3.get_text() if 'mary kinder' in text3.lower(): print("✓ Mary Kinder mentioned in Indiana History Blog") # Look for specific posts or articles articles = soup3.find_all(['article', 'div'], class_=lambda x: x and ('post' in x.lower() or 'entry' in x.lower())) relevant_articles = [] for article in articles: article_text = article.get_text() if 'mary kinder' in article_text.lower(): relevant_articles.append(article_text[:1000]) # First 1000 chars if relevant_articles: print(f"Found {len(relevant_articles)} relevant articles:") for k, article in enumerate(relevant_articles[:2], 1): print(f"\n--- Article {k} ---") print(article) findings.append({ 'source': 'Indiana History Blog Marion', 'url': url3, 'content': relevant_articles, 'type': 'government_blog', 'articles_found': len(relevant_articles) }) else: print("Mary Kinder mentioned but no specific articles extracted") else: print("No Mary Kinder references found") else: print(f"Could not access Indiana History Blog (Status: {response3.status_code})") except Exception as e: print(f"Error accessing Indiana History Blog: {str(e)}") time.sleep(2) # # First, let's inspect the FBI archival findings file to understand its structure import json import os print("=== INSPECTING FBI ARCHIVAL FINDINGS STRUCTURE ===") fbi_file = 'workspace/mary_kinder_archival_findings.json' if os.path.exists(fbi_file): with open(fbi_file, 'r') as f: fbi_data = json.load(f) print(f"File loaded successfully") print(f"Type: {type(fbi_data)}") print(f"Number of findings: {len(fbi_data)}") # Inspect structure of each finding for i, finding in enumerate(fbi_data): print(f"\nFinding {i+1}:") print(f" Keys: {list(finding.keys())}") print(f" Source: {finding.get('source', 'Unknown')}") print(f" Type: {finding.get('type', 'Unknown')}") if 'sections_found' in finding: print(f" Sections found: {finding['sections_found']}") else: print(f"File {fbi_file} does not exist") print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== ANALYZING FBI CONTENT FOR MARY KINDER TESTIMONY DETAILS ===") # Now analyze the FBI content specifically for testimony and legal proceedings if os.path.exists(fbi_file): # Look for FBI sections that mention Mary Kinder for finding in fbi_data: if finding.get('type') == 'fbi_archive' and 'content' in finding: print(f"\n--- Analyzing {finding['source']} ---") sections = finding['content'] for j, section in enumerate(sections, 1): print(f"\nFBI Section {j}:") print(f"Length: {len(section)} characters") # Look for key legal terms and testimony indicators legal_terms = ['testimony', 'witness', 'court', 'trial', 'arraigned', 'evidence', 'arrested', 'charged'] location_terms = ['tucson', 'arizona', 'indianapolis', 'lima', 'ohio'] gang_terms = ['dillinger', 'pierpont', 'clark', 'makley', 'gang'] found_terms = [] section_lower = section.lower() for term in legal_terms + location_terms + gang_terms: if term in section_lower: found_terms.append(term) if found_terms: print(f"Key terms found: {', '.join(found_terms)}") # Extract specific details about Mary Kinder's role if 'mary kinder' in section_lower: print(f"\n--- DETAILED CONTENT ---") print(section) # Save this section for further analysis section_filename = f'workspace/fbi_section_{j}_mary_kinder.txt' with open(section_filename, 'w') as f: f.write(f"FBI SECTION {j} - MARY KINDER REFERENCES\n") f.write("=" * 50 + "\n\n") f.write(section) print(f"\nSection saved to: {section_filename}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== SEARCHING FOR ADDITIONAL MARY KINDER TESTIMONY SOURCES ===") # Let's search for more specific information about Mary Kinder's testimony # Focus on court records and trial proceedings import requests api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: # Search for specific court testimony and trial records specific_queries = [ '"Mary Kinder" testimony "Harry Pierpont" "Sheriff Sarber" murder trial court', '"Mary Kinder" witness "state evidence" Pierpont Dillinger gang trial', '"Mary Kinder" arraigned Tucson Arizona 1934 testimony court proceedings', '"Mary Kinder" informant FBI cooperation Dillinger gang prosecution' ] all_new_results = [] for i, query in enumerate(specific_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SEARCH {i}: {query[:50]}... ---") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 8 } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Look for results that specifically mention testimony or court proceedings for result in results['organic_results']: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') url = result.get('link', '') combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() # Prioritize results with testimony/court references if any(term in combined_text for term in ['testimony', 'trial', 'court', 'witness', 'evidence']): print(f"\n PRIORITY RESULT:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {url}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") all_new_results.append({ 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'priority': 'high' }) else: print("No results found") else: print(f"Search failed: {response.status_code}") # Save new search results if all_new_results: with open('workspace/mary_kinder_testimony_search.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(all_new_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\n=== NEW SEARCH SUMMARY ===") print(f"Total priority results found: {len(all_new_results)}") print(f"Results saved to: workspace/mary_kinder_testimony_search.json") # Highlight most promising new sources print(f"\nMost promising new sources:") for i, result in enumerate(all_new_results[:5], 1): print(f"{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['url']}") else: print("No API key available for additional searches") print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===") print(f"Files created in workspace/:") print(f"- FBI section analysis files (fbi_section_*_mary_kinder.txt)") print(f"- New testimony search results (mary_kinder_testimony_search.json)") print(f"\nNext step: Examine specific FBI sections and new search results for testimony details")

# First, let's inspect the FBI archival findings file to understand its structure import json import os print("=== INSPECTING FBI ARCHIVAL FINDINGS STRUCTURE ===") fbi_file = 'workspace/mary_kinder_archival_findings.json' if os.path.exists(fbi_file): with open(fbi_file, 'r') as f: fbi_data = json.load(f) print(f"File loaded successfully") print(f"Type: {type(fbi_data)}") print(f"Number of findings: {len(fbi_data)}") # Inspect structure of each finding for i, finding in enumerate(fbi_data): print(f"\nFinding {i+1}:") print(f" Keys: {list(finding.keys())}") print(f" Source: {finding.get('source', 'Unknown')}") print(f" Type: {finding.get('type', 'Unknown')}") if 'sections_found' in finding: print(f" Sections found: {finding['sections_found']}") else: print(f"File {fbi_file} does not exist") print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== ANALYZING FBI CONTENT FOR MARY KINDER TESTIMONY DETAILS ===") # Now analyze the FBI content specifically for testimony and legal proceedings if os.path.exists(fbi_file): # Look for FBI sections that mention Mary Kinder for finding in fbi_data: if finding.get('type') == 'fbi_archive' and 'content' in finding: print(f"\n--- Analyzing {finding['source']} ---") sections = finding['content'] for j, section in enumerate(sections, 1): print(f"\nFBI Section {j}:") print(f"Length: {len(section)} characters") # Look for key legal terms and testimony indicators legal_terms = ['testimony', 'witness', 'court', 'trial', 'arraigned', 'evidence', 'arrested', 'charged'] location_terms = ['tucson', 'arizona', 'indianapolis', 'lima', 'ohio'] gang_terms = ['dillinger', 'pierpont', 'clark', 'makley', 'gang'] found_terms = [] section_lower = section.lower() for term in legal_terms + location_terms + gang_terms: if term in section_lower: found_terms.append(term) if found_terms: print(f"Key terms found: {', '.join(found_terms)}") # Extract specific details about Mary Kinder's role if 'mary kinder' in section_lower: print(f"\n--- DETAILED CONTENT ---") print(section) # Save this section for further analysis section_filename = f'workspace/fbi_section_{j}_mary_kinder.txt' with open(section_filename, 'w') as f: f.write(f"FBI SECTION {j} - MARY KINDER REFERENCES\n") f.write("=" * 50 + "\n\n") f.write(section) print(f"\nSection saved to: {section_filename}") print("\n" + "="*80) print("=== SEARCHING FOR ADDITIONAL MARY KINDER TESTIMONY SOURCES ===") # Let's search for more specific information about Mary Kinder's testimony # Focus on court records and trial proceedings import requests api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY") if api_key: # Search for specific court testimony and trial records specific_queries = [ '"Mary Kinder" testimony "Harry Pierpont" "Sheriff Sarber" murder trial court', '"Mary Kinder" witness "state evidence" Pierpont Dillinger gang trial', '"Mary Kinder" arraigned Tucson Arizona 1934 testimony court proceedings', '"Mary Kinder" informant FBI cooperation Dillinger gang prosecution' ] all_new_results = [] for i, query in enumerate(specific_queries, 1): print(f"\n--- SEARCH {i}: {query[:50]}... ---") params = { "q": query, "api_key": api_key, "engine": "google", "google_domain": "google.com", "safe": "off", "num": 8 } response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params) if response.status_code == 200: results = response.json() if results.get("organic_results"): print(f"Found {len(results['organic_results'])} results") # Look for results that specifically mention testimony or court proceedings for result in results['organic_results']: title = result.get('title', '') snippet = result.get('snippet', '') url = result.get('link', '') combined_text = f"{title} {snippet}".lower() # Prioritize results with testimony/court references if any(term in combined_text for term in ['testimony', 'trial', 'court', 'witness', 'evidence']): print(f"\n PRIORITY RESULT:") print(f" Title: {title}") print(f" URL: {url}") print(f" Snippet: {snippet}") all_new_results.append({ 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'priority': 'high' }) else: print("No results found") else: print(f"Search failed: {response.status_code}") # Save new search results if all_new_results: with open('workspace/mary_kinder_testimony_search.json', 'w') as f: json.dump(all_new_results, f, indent=2) print(f"\n=== NEW SEARCH SUMMARY ===") print(f"Total priority results found: {len(all_new_results)}") print(f"Results saved to: workspace/mary_kinder_testimony_search.json") # Highlight most promising new sources print(f"\nMost promising new sources:") for i, result in enumerate(all_new_results[:5], 1): print(f"{i}. {result['title']}") print(f" URL: {result['url']}") else: print("No API key available for additional searches") print(f"\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===") print(f"Files created in workspace/:") print(f"- FBI section analysis files (fbi_section_*_mary_kinder.txt)") print(f"- New testimony search results (mary_kinder_testimony_search.json)") print(f"\nNext step: Examine specific FBI sections and new search results for testimony details")
